# Test source

```ts
  4   | test.beforeEach(async ({ page }) => {
  5   |   await page.goto('https://www.imdb.com/chart/top/');
  6   | });
  7   | 
  8   | test.afterEach(async ({ page }) => {
  9   |     console.log('Test completed');
  10  | });
  11  | 
  12  |   // 1. Verify Top 250 page opens successfully
  13  |   test('Top 250 page opens', async ({ page }) => {
  14  |     await expect(page).toHaveURL(/top/);
  15  |   });
  16  | 
  17  |   // 2. Verify movie list is displayed
  18  |   test('Movie list is visible', async ({ page }) => {
  19  |     const movies = page.locator('li.ipc-metadata-list-summary-item');
  20  |     await expect(movies.first()).toBeVisible();
  21  |   });
  22  | 
  23  |   // 3. Verify ranking numbers are visible
  24  |   test('Ranking numbers are visible', async ({ page }) => {
  25  |     const rank = page.locator('h3').first();
  26  |     await expect(rank).toBeVisible();
  27  |   });
  28  | 
  29  |   // 4. Verify movie titles are displayed
  30  |   test('Movie titles are displayed', async ({ page }) => {
  31  |     const title = page.locator('h3').first();
  32  |     await expect(title).toContainText(/\w+/);
  33  |   });
  34  | 
  35  |   // 5. Verify movie ratings are visible
  36  |   test('Movie ratings are visible', async ({ page }) => {
  37  |     const rating = page.locator('[data-testid="ratingGroup--imdb-rating"]');
  38  |     await expect(rating.first()).toBeVisible();
  39  |   });
  40  | 
  41  |   // 6. Verify release years are shown
  42  |   test('Release year is displayed', async ({ page }) => {
  43  |     const year = page.locator('.cli-title-metadata');
  44  |     await expect(year.first()).toBeVisible();
  45  |   });
  46  | 
  47  |   // 7. storyline
  48  |   test('storyline is visible', async ({ page }) => {
  49  |     await page.getByRole('link', { name: '12 Angry Men', exact: true }).click();
  50  |     // await expect(page.getByTestId('Storyline')).toBeVisible();
  51  |     await expect(page.locator('body')).toContainText('Storyline');
  52  |   });
  53  | 
  54  |   // 8. Verify clicking movie opens detail page
  55  |   test('Open movie details page', async ({ page }) => {
  56  |     await page.locator('h3').first().click();
  57  |     await expect(page).toHaveURL(/title/);
  58  |   });
  59  | 
  60  |   // 9. user reviews
  61  |   test('User reviews are visible', async ({ page }) => {
  62  |     await page.goto('https://www.imdb.com/chart/top/');
  63  |     await page.getByRole('link', { name: '12 Angry Men', exact: true }).click();
  64  |     await page.getByTestId('hero-subnav-bar-topic-links').getByRole('link', { name: 'User reviews' }).click();
  65  |     await expect(page.getByText('User reviews12 Angry Men')).toBeVisible();
  66  |   });
  67  | 
  68  |   // 10. Verify ratings are valid values
  69  |   test('Ratings are valid', async ({ page }) => {
  70  |     const rating = await page.locator('[data-testid="ratingGroup--imdb-rating"]').first().textContent();
  71  |     expect(parseFloat(rating)).toBeGreaterThan(0);
  72  |   });
  73  | 
  74  |   // 11. Verify search within Top 250 works
  75  |   test('Search movie from Top 250', async ({ page }) => {
  76  |     await page.getByPlaceholder('Search IMDb').fill('The Dark Knight');
  77  |     await page.keyboard.press('Enter');
  78  |     await expect(page).toHaveURL(/find/);
  79  |   });
  80  | 
  81  |   // 12. Verify page scroll behavior
  82  |   test('Page scroll works', async ({ page }) => {
  83  |     await page.mouse.wheel(0, 3000);
  84  |     await page.waitForTimeout(2000);
  85  |   });
  86  | 
  87  |   // 13. Verify page reload keeps data intact
  88  |   test('Page reload works properly', async ({ page }) => {
  89  |     await page.reload();
  90  |     const movies = page.locator('li.ipc-metadata-list-summary-item');
  91  |     await expect(movies.first()).toBeVisible();
  92  |   });
  93  | 
  94  |   // 14. Verify no duplicate movie entries exist
  95  |   test('No duplicate movie titles', async ({ page }) => {
  96  |     const titles = await page.locator('h3').allTextContents();
  97  |     const uniqueTitles = [...new Set(titles)];
  98  |     expect(titles.length).toBe(uniqueTitles.length);
  99  |   });
  100 | 
  101 |   // 15. Verify URL is correct after navigation
  102 |   test('Correct URL after opening movie', async ({ page }) => {
  103 |     await page.locator('h3').nth(1).click();
> 104 |     await expect(page.url()).toContain('/title/');
      |                              ^ Error: expect(received).toContain(expected) // indexOf
  105 |   });
  106 | 
  107 | });
```
